<t>CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS customers (id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY, name TEXT, email TEXT, phone TEXT)</t><s>INSERT INTO customers (name, email, phone) VALUES ('John Doe', 'john.doe@example.com', '123-456-7890') ON CONFLICT (id) DO UPDATE SET name = 'John Doe', email = 'john.doe@example.com', phone = '123-456-7890';</s>

CREATE TABLE interactions (interaction_id INT PRIMARY KEY, lead_id INT, interaction_date TIMESTAMP, interaction_type VARCHAR, outcome VARCHAR);</t><s>INSERT INTO leads (lead_id, customer_id, campaign_id, lead_name, lead_email, status) VALUES (1, 1, 1, 'Jane Smith', 'jane.smith@example.com', 'New') ON CONFLICT (lead_id) DO UPDATE SET customer_id = 1, campaign_id = 1, lead_name = 'Jane Smith', lead_email = 'jane.smith@example.com', status = 'New';</s>

CREATE TABLE responses (response_id INT PRIMARY KEY, email_id INT, lead_id INT, response_type VARCHAR(20), response_date DATETIME)</t><s>upsert into customers (customer_id, name, email, phone) values (101, 'john doe', 'john.doe@example.com', '1234567890') on duplicate key update name = 'john doe', email = 'john.doe@example.com', phone = '1234567890';</s>

CREATE TABLE responses (response_id INT PRIMARY KEY, email_id INT, lead_id INT, response_type VARCHAR(20), response_date DATETIME)</t><s>upsert into customers (customer_id, name, email, phone) values (101, 'john doe', 'john.doe@example.com', '1234567890') on duplicate key update name = 'john doe', email = 'john.doe@example.com', phone = '1234567890';</s>

CREATE TABLE responses (response_id INT PRIMARY KEY, email_id INT, lead_id INT, response_type VARCHAR(20), response_date DATETIME)

CREATE TABLE leads (lead_id INT PRIMARY KEY, customer_id INT, campaign_id INT, status VARCHAR(20), source VARCHAR(50))</t><s>upsert into leads (lead_id, customer_id, campaign_id, status, source) values (301, 101, 201, 'new lead', 'website') on duplicate key update customer_id = 101, campaign_id = 201, status = 'new lead', source = 'website';</s>

CREATE TABLE customers (customer_id INT PRIMARY KEY, name VARCHAR(50), email VARCHAR(50), phone VARCHAR(15))

CREATE TABLE leads (lead_id INT PRIMARY KEY, customer_id INT, campaign_id INT, status VARCHAR(20), source VARCHAR(50))

CREATE TABLE responses (response_id INT PRIMARY KEY, email_id INT, lead_id INT, response_type VARCHAR(20), response_date DATETIME)</t><s>UPSERT INTO leads (lead_id, customer_id, campaign_id, status, source) VALUES (301, 101, 201, 'New Lead', 'Website') ON DUPLICATE KEY UPDATE customer_id = 101, campaign_id = 201, status = 'New Lead', source = 'Website';</s>

CREATE TABLE campaigns (campaign_id INT PRIMARY KEY, name VARCHAR(50), start_date DATE, end_date DATE, budget DECIMAL(10,2))

CREATE TABLE responses (response_id INT PRIMARY KEY, email_id INT, lead_id INT, response_type VARCHAR(20), response_date DATETIME)</t><s>upsert into leads (lead_id, customer_id, campaign_id, status, source) values (301, 101, 201, 'new lead', 'website') on duplicate key update customer_id = 101, campaign_id = 201, status = 'new lead', source = 'website';</s>

CREATE TABLE campaigns (campaign_id INT PRIMARY KEY, name VARCHAR(50), start_date DATE, end_date DATE, budget DECIMAL(10,2))

CREATE TABLE leads (lead_id INT PRIMARY KEY, customer_id INT, campaign_id INT, status VARCHAR(20), source VARCHAR(50))

CREATE TABLE customers (customer_id INT PRIMARY KEY, name VARCHAR(50), email VARCHAR(50), phone VARCHAR(15))</t><s>UPSERT INTO leads (lead_id, customer_id, campaign_id, status, source) VALUES (301, 101, 201, 'New Lead', 'Website') ON DUPLICATE KEY UPDATE customer_id = 101, campaign_id = 201, status = 'New Lead', source = 'Website';</s>
<t>CREATE TABLE responses (response_id INT PRIMARY KEY, email_id INT, lead_id INT, response_type VARCHAR(20), response_date DATETIME)

CREATE TABLE emails (email_id INT PRIMARY KEY, lead_id INT, subject VARCHAR(100), body TEXT, sent_date DATETIME)

CREATE TABLE campaigns (campaign_id INT PRIMARY KEY, name VARCHAR(50), start_date DATE, end_date DATE, budget DECIMAL(10,2))

CREATE TABLE leads (lead_id INT PRIMARY KEY, customer_id INT, campaign_id INT, status VARCHAR(20), source VARCHAR(50))

CREATE TABLE customers (customer_id INT PRIMARY KEY, name VARCHAR(50), email VARCHAR(50), phone VARCHAR(15))</t><s>upsert into leads (lead_id, customer_id, campaign_id, status, source) values (301, 101, 201, 'new lead', 'website') on duplicate key update customer_id = 101, campaign_id = 201, status = 'new lead', source = 'website';</s>
